( ) de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsang ba bstan pa'i dbang du byas (tshu) nas @# / /
bskal ba bzang po'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gzugs kyi sku dang dam pa'i chos la bsrung ba la rnam pa thams cad du bdag por byas pa yin pa'i phyir dang /
phyag na rdo rje dbang bskur ba la sogs pa las bstan pa gtad pa yin pa'i phyir dang /
gzhan rnams kyis khyad par brjod pa med pa'i phyir na lcang lo can na bzhugs pa'i sa bcu'i dbang phyug rdo rje 'dzin pa chen pos 'jig rten thams cad rjes su bzung ba'i phyir /
zhes sogs kyis gzhan lugs bkod cing /
gzhan dag ni 'di nyid kyi yongs su gtad pa'i le'u las /
zhes sogs kyis rang lugs bstan te /
'di skad bdag gis thos pa zhes bka' sdud pa po gang yin la rtsod pa'o / /
de la pha rol po'i 'dod tshul ni /
gsang ba bstan pa'am gsang ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i mdos bshad tshul gyi dbang du byas na 'ang phyag rdor sdud pa po yin la /
phyag na rdo rje dbang bskur ba'i rgyud ltar na'ang de yin te /
snga ma'i tshul ni sngon sangs rgyas stong 'khor bsgyur yul 'khor srung gi sras su 'khrungs te thugs bskyed pa'i tshe de thams cad kyis bstan pa'i dbag por smon lam btab pa'i khye'u chos sems ni phyag rdor lin la /
chos 'khor bskur bar smon lam btab pa'i khye'u chos kyi blo gros ni tshangs pa gtsug phud can yin pa'i phyir dang /
des smon lam 'grub pa'i phyir /
phyag na rdo rje dbang bskur ba las kyang phyag rdor chos kyi rgyal bor mnga' gsol ba'i phyir sdud pa yin no / /

spang gnyen gnyis cig car mdzo sbrel g.yang la lhung ba ltar 'gag pa ni 'gag 'gyur gyi spong lugs so / /
na bdag nyid chen po zhes 'dug pas blo ldan shes rab yin nam dpyod /
(196pa) gser 'phreng las 'di byang ye'i bzhed par bshad do / /
(200ba) mngon mtho la ltos nas kyang der nges /
(le4) mdo sde rgyan las /
longs spyod dang lus phun sum tshogs pa dang / /
'khor rtsom phun sum tshogs pa mngon mtho dang / /
rtag tu nyon mongs dbang nyid mi 'gro dang / /
bya ba rnams la phyin ci ma log pa'o / /
'di @# / /
mngon mtho la ltos pa'i drang nges sgrub byed dang /
( ) don gnyis sgrub pas kyang der nges /
(she4) 'di'i sgrub byed /
sems can don ni rab brtson pa'i / /
gtong ngang mi gnod bzod bas byed / /
gnas dang grol ba gzhir bcas pa / /
rang don rnam pa thams cad pa'o / /
zhes gsungs /
( ) gzhan don rnam pa thams cad pas kyang der nges /
(se4) 'di'i sgrub byed /
mi 'phongs pa dang rnam par mi 'tshe dang / /
rnam 'tshe bzod dang bya bas mi skyo dang / /
dga' byed legs par brjod pa de yi phyir / /
gzhan gyi don ni rang gi don yin no / /
zhes gsungs /
( ) theg chen thams cad sdud pas kyang der nges /
(he4) 'di'i sgrub byed /
longs spyod mngon par mi dga' dang / /
rab gus gnyis la mi skyo dang / /
rnam 'byed rnam par mi rtog pa / /
theg chen mtha' dag 'dir zad do / /
zhes gsungs /
( ) thabs kyi rnam pa thams cad pa'i dbang du byas kyang der nges /
(e4) 'di'i sgrub byed /
yul rnams la ni ma chags lam / /
de thob rnam g.yeng sdom pa'i gzhan / /
sems can mi gtong 'phel ba dang / /
sgrib pa rnam par sbyong ba'i gzhan / /
zhes gsungs /
(201pa) rgyu dang /
rnam smin dang /
smon lam dang /
so sor rtogs pa'i sgom pa bzhi dang /
(ko4) sgom tshul gyi nang gses dbye ba 'di dag la rtsa tshig med kyang /
dbyig 'grel gsal /
( ) lnga pa dbang 'byor la sku ngo bo nyid sku longs sku dang /
spyod pa sprul sku dang /
ston pa phyin drug la dbang 'byor pa sgom pa gsum rnams yod pa'i phyir te /
( ) phyin drug re re la ngo bo nyid dang /
rgyu dang /
'bras bu dang /
las dang /
sbyor ba dang /
'jug pa dang drug gi sgo nas rab tu dbye ba de yin pa'i phyir te /
rgyan las /
sbyin pa la sbyar na /
don rnams gtong bar byed pa dang /
(kho4) 'dis ngo bo / /
rtsa ba sems pa la brten pa / /
'dis rgyu /
lus dang longs spyod phun tshogs dang / /
'dis 'bras bu /
gnyis rjes 'dzin dang rdzogs byed dang / /
'dis las /
de yang ser sna med ldan dang / /
'dis ldan pa /
chos dang zang zing mi 'jigs gtong / /
'dis 'jug pa'i khyad par bstan zhes dbyig 'grel gsung /
( ) bdun pa mi mthun phyogs nyams par byas tshul yod de /
mi mthun phyogs (go4) longs spyod la chags pa /
phyi bshol la chags pa /
mchog 'dzin la chags pa /
lan la chags pa /
rnam smin la chags pa /
mi mthun phyogs la chags pa /
rnam g.yeng la chags pa ste /
( ) chags pa bdun ci rigs las grol ba'i phyir te /
(203na) brgyad pa phar phyin gyi yon tan rgya che la ngo mtshar ba rang gzhan gyi dga' bde bla na med pa yod de /
so so'i yon tan tshigs bcad nyer gnyis kyis bshad pa'i phyir te /
rgyan las /
sangs rgyas sras rnams (ngo4) 'dir tshigs bcad nyer gnyis dang /
dbyig 'grel du nyer gsum byung yang rtsa bar tshigs bcad so drug 'dug pas bsdu lugs dpyad dgos /
( ) zhes sogs nas /
brtson 'grus ldan pa thob pas pham pa med / /
ces pa'i bar 'byung ba'i phyir / / / /
'dir shog @# / /
grangs dang thig 'phreng gi ang yig rnams dang /
nyin srib kyi rtags su na yig dang ba yig 'jog dgos rnams /
bkra shis 'khyil gyi phar phyin skabs dang po'i par rnying dang bstun tshe /
der shog grangs kyi kha yig nor yod ba rnams kyang ma bcos par /
de dang mthun par par du brkos pa lags so / / / /
